- рЯЪЂ DevOps: Git ignore

- вЪЩпЄП Config: YAML files
- рЯР≥ DevOps: Docker files
- рЯМР Web: HTML files
- рЯУЦ Docs: Markdown files
- рЯУД Docs: Text files
- рЯО® Styles: Stylesheets
- рЯЦЉпЄП Assets: PNG images
- рЯЦЉпЄП Assets: JPEG images
- рЯУЬ JavaScript: JavaScript files
- рЯО® Assets: SVG images
- рЯФ§ Assets: TrueType fonts
- рЯФ§ Assets: Web fonts
- вЪЩпЄП Config: XML files

### Importance Levels
- рЯФі Critical: Essential project files
- рЯЯ° High: Important configuration files
- рЯФµ Medium: Helpful but not essential files
